File Format:

1. This summary section

  a. A separator line (================)
  b. The file path (File: path/to/file)

  d. The full contents of the file
  e. A blank line

Usage Guidelines:
-----------------
- This file should be treated as read-only. Any changes should be made to the
  original repository files, not this packed version.
- When processing this file, use the file path to distinguish
  between different files in the repository.
- Be aware that this file may contain sensitive information. Handle it with
  the same level of security as you would the original repository.

using Microsoft.UI.Xaml;
using Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Controls;
using Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Controls.Primitives;
using Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Data;
using Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Input;
using Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Media;
using Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Navigation;
using Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Shapes;
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices.WindowsRuntime;
using Windows.ApplicationModel;
using Windows.ApplicationModel.Activation;
using Windows.Foundation;
using Windows.Foundation.Collections;

// To learn more about WinUI, the WinUI project structure,
// and more about our project templates, see: http://aka.ms/winui-project-info.

namespace MusicAF
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Provides application-specific behavior to supplement the default Application class.
    /// </summary>
    public partial class App : Application
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Initializes the singleton application object.  This is the first line of authored code
        /// executed, and as such is the logical equivalent of main() or WinMain().
        /// </summary>
        public App()
        {
            this.InitializeComponent();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Invoked when the application is launched.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="args">Details about the launch request and process.</param>
        protected override void OnLaunched(Microsoft.UI.Xaml.LaunchActivatedEventArgs args)
        {
            m_window = new MainWindow();
            m_window.Activate();
        }

        private Window m_window;
    }
}

// and more about our project templates, see: http://aka.ms/winui-project-info.

    /// An empty window that can be used on its own or navigated to within a Frame.
    /// </summary>

    {

        {

            MainFrame.Navigate(typeof(MyLibraryPage));

        private global::Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Markup.IXamlMember CreateXamlMember(string longMemberName)
        {
            global::MusicAF.MusicAF_XamlTypeInfo.XamlMember xamlMember = null;
            global::MusicAF.MusicAF_XamlTypeInfo.XamlUserType userType;

            switch (longMemberName)
            {
            case "Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Controls.XamlControlsResources.UseCompactResources":
                userType = (global::MusicAF.MusicAF_XamlTypeInfo.XamlUserType)GetXamlTypeByName("Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Controls.XamlControlsResources");
                xamlMember = new global::MusicAF.MusicAF_XamlTypeInfo.XamlMember(this, "UseCompactResources", "Boolean");
                xamlMember.SetIsDependencyProperty();
                xamlMember.Getter = get_0_XamlControlsResources_UseCompactResources;
                xamlMember.Setter = set_0_XamlControlsResources_UseCompactResources;
